  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_7c782ef0-a1b0-4eef-8869-db477a2730d0'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

  <span id="freeText5968911788418753044" style="display:none">Young interior designer Ava O’Shea has an appointment for a first consultation at The Manor with the owner, Mr Jesse Ward. She is expecting nothing more than an overweight, cravat wearing, well-to-do countryman, and on arrival, nothing would suggest otherwise. How wrong could she be? This Man is devastatingly handsome, charming and confident. He is also a conceited, hedonistic playboy, who knows no boundaries. Ava desperately does not want to be attracted to him, but she can’t control the overwhelming effect he has on her. Every instinct is telling her to run, so she does, but Jesse Ward is not so willing to let her go. He wants her and is determined to have her. She knows she is heading for heartbreak, but how can she run when he won’t let her?</span>

<div class='allCommunityAnswers'>
<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/39959323-super-beta-reader"><img alt="" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_100x100-6433b08cbe793211f55e184d39e84c4d.png" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/39959323-super-beta-reader">Super*BETA*Reader</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Forget all the reviews. When you read a book like this, you need to keep in mind that it is fiction. JEM is not promoting abuse, she is writing about <a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Forget all the reviews. When you read a book like this, you need to keep in mind that it is fiction. JEM is not promoting abuse, she is writing about a flawed character. I don't know about you, but I'd find it terribly boring if I only read books about perfect men, who had perfect relationships and perfect everything. Of course Jesse is over the top and completely unreasonable etc. but just because that is what the main character is like doesn't mean it's automatically a bad book. I thoroughly enjoyed the series, but you must be warned, you will only truly understand why he is the way he is when you get right to the end of the third book. It's not an excuse for his behavior, but it certainly does explain why he is so controlling and paranoid when it comes to Ava. I can understand why people who haven't finished the series feel so frustrated. It's definitely worth a read though.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>
</div>

But I felt nothing here in this book.<br><br>I wanted to dump the book in the middle, but I kept going only for the end and even that didn't live up to any shit. I have a feeling even that will be dragged if the author wants to move stuff into the 3rd book.<br><br>Sarah was a bitch, Jesse is fucking dumb and Ava is so bloody pissing off and stupid. <div id="review_469047437" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/469047437" />
    <a title="Britt" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2196186-britt"><img alt="Britt" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1349958146p2/2196186.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/469047437?book_show_action=true">Dec 03, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Britt" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Britt" href="/user/show/2196186-britt">Britt</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer469047437" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15084726681886984230">No, No and just No. <br/><br/>This book was sort of like watching a car crash about to happen. You can see it happening right in front of you and it’s not something pleasant you want to experience, but for the hell of it you can’t bring yourself to look away. <br/><br/>There are just so many problems with this book (I even wrote a damn list), so I am apologising in advance if this review gets a bit ranty.<br/> <br/><u> 5 reasons why I hated this book</u><br/><br/><b> 1. Jesse’s possessiveness. </b> <br/>I have experienced my fair share of super alpha ma</span>
  <span id="freeText15084726681886984230" style="display:none">No, No and just No. <br /><br />This book was sort of like watching a car crash about to happen. You can see it happening right in front of you and it’s not something pleasant you want to experience, but for the hell of it you can’t bring yourself to look away. <br /><br />There are just so many problems with this book (I even wrote a damn list), so I am apologising in advance if this review gets a bit ranty.<br /> <br /><u> 5 reasons why I hated this book</u><br /><br /><b> 1. Jesse’s possessiveness. </b> <br />I have experienced my fair share of super alpha males. Despite some negative reviews I enjoyed Christian Grey, Gideon Cross, James Cavendish and even Travis Maddox (oh the horror I know). However I could not deal with Jesse Ward. Whilst Christian may be possessive of Ana in Fifty Shades he still lets her go to work and most of his possessiveness stems from the fact that she is actually in real danger. If Jesse had his way Ava would never leave his sight, he doesn’t like her to work, even going as far as coming into her work and trying to buy all her time and mark time in for every day in her daily planner. He gets bouncers to watch her when she goes out with friends and makes her promise not to drink. He leaves 8 missed calls while she is in the damn shower, and when they are fighting she wakes up to find 42 missed calls from him. Hello Ava, that’s called a stalker not a lover. <br /><br />Secondly he seems to have a huge hypocritical problem with Ava’s swearing while swearing like a trooper himself. This just pissed me the FUCK off. <br /><br /><b> 2. Ava’s stupidity </b><br />What’s worse about this book is that Ava acknowledges that Jesse is crazy, controlling and stubborn; she understands it is not healthy behaviour that he is crazy but she accepts it anyways. <br /><br /><b> “What I’ve just sustained should repulse me, but it doesn’t. I’d do anything for him.” </b><br /><br />Why doesn’t she just leave? Probably because he won’t let her. Oh and the fact that she thinks he is perfect. The way she describes his perfection made me want to gag. Lines like these:<br /><br /><b> “This man is so perfect, I’m almost in pain.”<br /><br /> “Good god, he is way past perfect.” </b><br /><br />GET A GRIP ON YOURSELF WOMAN!!!<br /><br /><b> 3. The plot, or lack thereof </b><br />This book basically goes along the lines of something like this:<br />Ava and Jesse fuck, then she runs away and ignores her phone while he leaves a bazillion messages and calls a bazillion times. Then he chases her down and gives what he dubs (yes he does) a ‘sense fuck’ and she forgots the reason why she ran away in the first place. This happens again and again without them ever communicating about what was the issue in the first place. They don’t talk about it, they just start having sex again. Jesse doesn’t ask what made Ava run, Ava doesn’t try and discuss her insecurities with Jesse. It’s a bloody train wreck. Oh and did I mention that this same scenario happens three or four times throughout the book?. Its repetitive, annoying and predictable. There is this big secret that we all guessed in the first 10% that finally comes to fruition at the end of the book and that’s about it. <br /><br /><b> 4. The great unsexiness (and just plain stupid). </b><br />There are just parts of this book that made me laugh at their stupidity, made no logistical sense and didn’t seem realistic or sexy. <br /><br />-The first time that Jesse and Ava have sex, Ava lets him do something <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ anal sex  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> that seemed a bit unrealistic to happen on the first date. She just acknowledged a few pages ago that she wouldn’t let her boyfriend of four years do that but she just jumps in and lets Jesse do it when they have only just had sex. It seems very unrealistic. <br /><br />-At 28% Ava tells Jesse she really needs to go to the toilet but he instead pins her down and she lets him have her way with him. HELLO??? They obviously have never heard of something called a urinary tract infection!<br /><br />-Also quotes like this didn’t really make me hot and heavy<br /><br /><b> "I’m panting like a dehydrated dog" </b> hmmm sexy Ava<br /><br /><b> "I’m gagging for him." </b> Yes Ava you should be gagging, he is disgusting but I don’t think this is what this sentence is meant to mean. It’s probably some Brit slang that I am oblivious to but it didn’t really invoke the sexiest visuals. <br /><br /><b> 5. The editing (or lack thereof) </b><br />I understand this this is a self-published novel but some of the editing in this book was so bad. <br /><br /><b> "How long have you been stood here."<br />	<br />"I see him stood watching me."<br /></b><br /><br />Ok somebody needs to teach Jodi the difference between stood and standing. <br /><br /><b> “with everything else I have to poke up with.” </b> I think she means put. <br /><br />I usually don’t notice bad editing as much as a lot of other reviewers do but I couldn’t miss this one. <br /><br />SORRY TO EVERYONE WHO LOVED IT! But this book just was not for me. <br /><br />That said I probably will torture myself with the second book, because as I said I can’t look away from the car crash. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15084726681886984230" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/454563271" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/454563271?book_show_action=true">Nov 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer454563271" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12264678585831231196">I'm torn on how to rate this book. I liked some of it, I disliked some of it, some of it was thrilling, some of it was frustrating so...<br/><br/><b> 3.5 stars. </b><br/><br/>This book has been 'going around' a lot and I was very intrigued by the controlling, possessive billionaire premise. <br/><br/><b> <i> “Just tell me one thing before you leave, Ava.” His voice prickles at my senses… His face is serious, but still stunning. “How loud do you think you’ll scream when I fuck you?” </i> </b><br/><br/>I’m not a fan of comparing books, I prefer to let each </span>
  <span id="freeText12264678585831231196" style="display:none">I'm torn on how to rate this book. I liked some of it, I disliked some of it, some of it was thrilling, some of it was frustrating so...<br><br><b> 3.5 stars. </b><br><br>This book has been 'going around' a lot and I was very intrigued by the controlling, possessive billionaire premise. <br><br><b> <i> “Just tell me one thing before you leave, Ava.” His voice prickles at my senses… His face is serious, but still stunning. “How loud do you think you’ll scream when I fuck you?” </i> </b><br><br>I’m not a fan of comparing books, I prefer to let each one stand on its own. But in the case of this book, after the huge impact of the last 2 mega-successful controlling billionaire series, its inevitable that some comparisons will be made. But, personally, if I were to do so, I honestly feel like Jesse was maybe a bit more like a non-kinky Knight than Christian or Gideon.<br><br>Let’s start out from the beginning. Because I felt differently about this book in the beginning than I did at the end.<br><br>To say that the beginning melted my panties and set my heart a-flutter is a mega understatement. I swear, after their first meeting, I was ready to just throw a 6 star rating at the book. I was hooked and utterly captivated by their chemistry.<br><br>When Ava, an up-and-coming interior designer lands a job at The Manor in the country side, the last thing she expects is for the proprietor, or Lord of the Manor, to be drop dead gorgeous. He is beyond intense and she is so strongly affected by him that he just takes over her mind every time she sees him. She jumps to several conclusions about him and decided though that its all too much for her and walks away. But Jesse is not one to be deterred from getting what he wants. He relentlessly peruses her until finally the combination of his determination and her intense desire for him make her give in.<br><br><i> <b> “I’m sorry,” he whispers softly… “I lied, I’m sorry. I told you, I can’t stay away… I need to have all of you, Ava. Say I can have all of you.” </b></i> <br><br>Jesse gave me shivers!!! He was a gorgeous, controlling, domineering, self-assured British billionaire with a husky accent. I mean, holy hell, can you just picture that?? *fans self* But… he was also an unreasonable control freak and pretty much a stalker. I do love me a controlling, possessive hero but… I felt he went too far. Even I was feeling stifled and I wasn’t the object of his attention.<br><br>He was just … too much sometimes… like too stalker-ish, too rude, too demanding, too extreme, too unreasonable, too neurotic, borderline immature (especially at the end). And Ava just gave in every time. I wish she stood up a bit more.<br><br>And honestly, if he told her to <i> “Watch your mouth!” </i> <u> one </u> more time… *mimes throttling* . I mean, its not like he was a saint or anything. He swore all the time, but every time she’d swear at all, he’d yell at her. Every. Time. It got old real fast.<br><br>Let’s just say that, in real life, I’d personally actually put up with a Christian or a Gideon, but a Jesse would have been kicked to the fucking curb if he said/did the things he did in this book to me. That being said, this is fiction. And, in the spirit of appreciating him for the fictional character that he is, I tried to be more lenient in my judgement.<br><br>But I guess I just found Jesse too extreme overall. At the same time, I really did like him and felt like I wanted to know where his story went, but I couldn’t really look past a few of his demands.<br><br>Ava. hmmm I don’t know what to say about her. I didn’t like a lot of what she did but at the same time, I didn’t dislike her. She didn’t make me mad or anything, but her actions/reactions just didn’t make me admire her. First of all, I’m really surprised she didn’t see the “twist” at the end. I had my suspicions from the beginning and after that, there was a lot that hinted at it and she never had a clue. Second, I didn’t like how, on her own she was an intelligent, relatively strong, independent woman, but the second she shared the same air as Jesse, she pretty much turned into a doormat. So many moments when he’d say things to her like <i> “Who has the power?” </i>, I really just wanted her, at some point, to stand up to him, but she completely gave in every time. Even when she did “rebel”, it was always relatively short-lived. <br><br>I felt that Jesse took things to an extreme and what would have been needed to balance him out was someone that wouldn’t like outright defy him per say, but that would have stood on her own enough to not give him complete and utter power.<br><br>Also, with many other such controlling, possessive heroes, I guess what makes me accept them so readily, is that, no matter what extremes they’ll go to to control their women, they are still always thinking of the woman first. But there were several times here where I felt that Jesse put his need to control her above her comfort.<br><br>There are a few examples, but the one I’ll reference is the scene at 25%. I found it very unrealistic and unbelievable. I don’t have any problem with butt sex – if its done well. But the fact that it was her first time doing it, that it was only their second time having sex at all, that she wasn’t even like ‘looking forward’ to it and then he just rammed her so suddenly like that (and that was after it was made very clear how well-endowed he was)…. I didn’t like how he handled it. I mean sure the scene was hot, and she did enjoy it in the end but I guess it was about as un-realistic as their always-perfectly-timed mutual orgasms… lol, I felt sometime like they were taking a photo or something “three…two…one…COME!” o_O<br><br>This book takes place in England and has a LOT of “Bristishisms” –&gt; Sodding. Knickers. Jumper. Quiff. Plum. Posh. Tart. Tube. Lush. Dribble. Bloody. Tosser. Bin bags. Knackered. Bird. Shag. Cheeky fag… there’s a lot. It didn’t bother me or anything, this isn’t a complaint, but it definitely jumps out at you.<br><br>The plot wasn’t overly gripping. The whole story was about them figuring each other out. Again, it wasn’t bad, I just didn’t feel like there was too much change in the characters by the end of the book and wasn’t really sure if the story had gone anywhere except at the very end.<br><br>There was only one thing in the books that really made me mad. Now, I understand that this book came out after Fifty Shades and that it’s got to fight to be appreciated on its own terms and not be labeled a copy or a wanna-be. But regardless, there IS the blatant fact that it is in a similar genre and, although it did stand on its own, it is without a doubt along the same lines and as such, given the context, I did <u> NOT</u> appreciate the blatant dig at putting down Dominants. I thought it was petty and disrespectful because there is <u> NO </u> doubt what was being referred to there. I hope that if this book ever gets published officially (currently, it is self-published) that that line gets taken out.<br><br>That being said, you should know that this is not a BDSM book. In fact, Jesse is relatively anti-kink. Its all straight-up, albeit intense, vanilla sex.<br><br>Parts of this book thrilled me and excited me. Parts of this book annoyed me and frustrated me. I’m torn here because I know a lot of people rated it with 5 stars. But I’m just trying to really be honest and something about the book didn’t fully sit right with me. At the same time, I did like it. I really did. I didn’t hate it. Please don’t think I hated it. Its not a bad book. I just had some issues with it.<br><br>It really helped that Jesse was totally hot. And when he wasn’t being overly control-y and stalker-y, I could really see myself falling for him. He had him moments of tender and sweet to be sure and I really did get the feeling like he was just out of his league with this relationship.<br><br><i> <b> “I want to look after you forever,” he whispers, pressing his lips against my temple.” </b></i> <br><br>I am intrigued by him. I do want to know more about his past. Where did he get that scar?? How old is he???? What happened in his past to make him so utterly terrified of loosing her? There are a lot of questions still to be answered and I’ll definitely be going on to the next book. I hope he gets over some things though in it. I didn’t feel like he ‘grew’ at all as a person in this story. In fact, you could almost say it ended on a major low point for him. So I’m really, really hoping that in the second book (that is supposed to be out in December, so thankfully not too long a wait) he makes some progress at learning to be more reasonable and finding a more balanced way of being controlling and possessive.<br><br>CASTING: <br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379799521i/655936._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> "This man is so perfect, I'm almost in pain. His dirty blond hair looks like he's half attempted to get it into a semblance of a style but given up. His eyes are sludgy green, but bright and way too intense, and the stubble covering his square jaw does nothing to conceal the handsome features beneath it. He's lightly tanned and just... Oh God, he's devastating." </i><br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="12264678585831231196" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_482928478" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/482928478" />
    <a title="Miss H" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15490946-miss-h"><img alt="Miss H" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475977422p2/15490946.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/482928478?book_show_action=true">Dec 22, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Miss H" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Miss H" href="/user/show/15490946-miss-h">Miss H</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16139502-this-man">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=needs-proper-editing">needs-proper-editing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=insta-love-or-insta-lust">insta-love-or-insta-lust</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=drama-llama">drama-llama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=hated-this-book">hated-this-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=insufferable-mc">insufferable-mc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=cheating-cheaters-who-cheat">cheating-cheaters-who-cheat</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=spineless-doormat-heroine">spineless-doormat-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=hero-unfaithful">hero-unfaithful</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=badly-written">badly-written</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer482928478" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8633720434299871620">This will most likely contain spoilers, so if that isn't your thing, feel free to ignore this review entirely.<br/><br/>I don't even know where to start. To be honest, I’m baffled by the amount of reviews that rave about how good this book is.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/414916.gif' width='282' height='150' alt='' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I mean, I just—I can’t.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/624071.gif' width='245' height='148' alt='' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>But to each their own, as they say. <br/><br/>The editing—well, this book could use a good editor. And that's to say nothing about the writing itself, which was bland, pedestrian, and long-winded.<br/><br/><u>
  <b>Jesse:</b>
</u><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401655ra/779861.gif' width='400' height='175' alt='' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401655ra/779862.gif' width='400' height='175' alt='' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398171ra/769273.gif' width='400' height='224' alt='' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I typically enjoy reading books with alpha male </span>
  <span id="freeText8633720434299871620" style="display:none">This will most likely contain spoilers, so if that isn't your thing, feel free to ignore this review entirely.<br><br>I don't even know where to start. To be honest, I’m baffled by the amount of reviews that rave about how good this book is.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/414916.gif" width="282" height="150" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I mean, I just—I can’t.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/624071.gif" width="245" height="148" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But to each their own, as they say. <br><br>The editing—well, this book could use a good editor. And that's to say nothing about the writing itself, which was bland, pedestrian, and long-winded.<br><br><u>
  <b>Jesse:</b>
</u><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401655ra/779861.gif" width="400" height="175" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401655ra/779862.gif" width="400" height="175" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398171ra/769273.gif" width="400" height="224" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I typically enjoy reading books with alpha male characters. It's sexy for a man to be a little possessive, especially in the bedroom. However, it is not okay when he tries to control every single aspect of your life, thus controlling <i>you</i>. There is a very thin line and it was crossed. Jesse is...well, he's beyond crazy. He’s a domineering, overly possessive control freak. And that's putting it nicely. There's nothing sexy about the way he behaves. The guy seriously has issues. He claims he only acts like a psycho around Ava. I find this hard to believe. He’s also really secretive about his age. He’s supposedly 30-ish. He sure as hell doesn’t act like a mature adult. He’s manipulative and uses sex as a weapon (or a "reminder", as he calls it). He has absolutely no regard for Ava’s feelings about anything. He does what he wants, when he wants.<br><br><blockquote>1: <i>He scowls at me good and proper. ‘Like I said, I don’t have to explain myself to you. Let’s go.’</i>
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>2: <i>‘Hey. Let’s get one thing straight, lady. You don’t dictate when and where I kiss you, or for how long.’ He’s deadly serious.</i>
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>3: <i>‘Listen to me, lady. You’re not going anywhere. I’ve told you repeatedly, so get fucking use to it!’</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Don't even get me started on his stalker tendencies. He calls Ava multiple times a day. Heaven forbid she not answer his call on the first ring. He calls and sends text messages and when that doesn't work, he shows up unannounced, demanding to know where she's been.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>‘I’m outside Kate’s kicking the door down,’ he snaps, ‘Is it too much to ask that you answer your phone the first time I call you?’<br><br>[...]<br><br>‘I was in the shower.’ <br><br>‘Well, take your phone next time.’ he orders.</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399702ra/773818.gif" width="400" height="144" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jesse has little to no redeeming qualities whatsoever, especially not after what happened at the end of the book. Ava finally grows a pair and he loses his shit, blaming her for the sorry state in which he finds himself. I fail to see how his choices and deplorable actions are anyone's fault but his own. It’s like, damn, get your act together!<br><br><u>
  <b>Ava:</b>
</u><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396194ra/763474.gif" width="300" height="135" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/613313.gif" width="400" height="299" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380371057ra/724056.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ava…yeah, I don’t even know where to begin with her. She’s a 26-year-old woman, but you’d never know that based on how she behaves. She's incredibly immature. She works as an interior designer, but she has got to be the most unprofessional person on the planet. <br><br>She's such a doormat, too. She repeatedly tells Jesse "no", but she doesn't really put her foot down. Jesse is a bully and she lets him get away with it. I mean, Jesse is one big unknown. She's curious, has questions, but does she ask them? No, of course not.<br><br>As for the supporting characters, the only one I'm going to mention is Kate. That woman, I swear. She's just as bad as Jesse. She and Ava are roommates, by the way. Ava tells her that she no longer wants to see Jesse and what does Kate do? She goes behind Ava's back, making deals with Jesse, allowing him into their apartment. Ava needs to seriously reevaluate their friendship, because Kate is a terrible friend.<br><br>The book itself was really drawn out. All the petty conflicts through miscommunication and misunderstandings was overdone and got on my nerves. It became redundant after a while. He’d make some unreasonable demand, she’d fight him on it, then he would proceed to “fuck some sense into her." Rinse and repeat. Unfortunately, if you remove all the unnecessary, contrived drama, you're not left with much of a story. With Jesse hiding Ava's birth control pills, I can only assume where book two is headed. Seriously, how dense can she be? "Oh, I can't find my pills." Yeah, that's because your psycho boyfriend stole them not once, but twice.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8633720434299871620" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

Their story is filled with covert pasts and hidden agendas! It’s truly a wild, bumpy and emotional ride loaded with intrigue and shockers, undiluted lust and mind-bending sex plus a compulsive and intense love. Be prepared to be swept away by their story!<br><br><u>Books in This Man series should be read in order:</u><br><b>Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/484476053" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">This Man</a><br>Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/489155223" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Beneath This Man</a><br>Book 3: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/509586014" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">This Man Confessed</a><br>Book 4: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2137108028" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">With This Man</a></b><br><br><b>This Man (book 1) opens up with Jesse Ward</b> needing 10 rooms decorated at a country estate, the Manor. He has specifically <b>requested Ava O’Shea</b> though she has to prior knowledge of him.   <span id="freeText1124268120690300611" style="display:none"><b> MOVE OVER 50 SHADES OF GREY TRILOGY AND CROSSFIRE SERIES...<br>THERE'S A NEW STEAMY TRILOGY IN TOWN! </b><br><br>I'm adding "This Man" to my list of favorites. Nothing matters – I still love<br>you."  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Now,<br><br><b> <u> Jesse </u></b> <br>Mr. Unreasonable Control Freak. STALKER MUCH? Like, don't you have a job? HAHA.<br>Sometimes, I also wanna scream because he won't open up on Ava. He's full of mystery. <br>But, you know what, I still love him. I need to know what’s standing in my way, if anything." </i><br><br>VS.<br><br>Ava and Jesse's:<br><i> "How loud do you think you’ll scream<br>when I fuck you?" </i><br><br>And that's both like in their second or third meeting. The chemistry between Jesse and Ava are way off the charts! I laughed, I cried, I got angry. The sex is great (there are tons, btw). It also annoys me how everytime Ava cusses, Jesse always tells her <i> "Watch your fucking mouth!" </i> like all throughout the book. UGH. The ending isn't what I expected though (coz I didn't know this was a trilogy). Anyway, at the end of the book, you will get some of your questions answered, but, I still got quite a few ones like: <i> What is really Sarah's role in Jesse's life? What's the story behind his scars? </i> and the ultimate question, <b> HOW OLD IS JESSE??? </b> Hopefully, we'll get the answers on book 2!<br><br><b> Overall, </b> I think this book was awesome, wonderfully written and HOT HOT HOT!!! Definitely worth reading! :)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397387ra/766723.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> 4.5 UNREASONABLY SMEXY STARS! </b><br><br><b> <u> UPDATE </u></b> <br><b> --&gt; Beneath This Man (This Man #2) Release Date: January 18, 2013 </b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13805863234537535997"><br/><b> 4.5 Cray-Cray - Wine Bottles & Mini Dresses & Countdowns to Zero & Eclairs</b><br/><b>
  <pre>
    <u>May I present to you... *drum roll*... My Jesse!</u>
  </pre>
</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397504i/767078._SY540_.jpg' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Holy sh!t to the crazy man - Jesse. I did not say that)<br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397504i/767081._SX540_.jpg' width='440' height='277' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The beautiful, young and ta</span>
  <span id="freeText13805863234537535997" style="display:none"><br><b> 4.5 Cray-Cray - Wine Bottles &amp; Mini Dresses &amp; Countdowns to Zero &amp; Eclairs</b><br><b>
  <pre>
    <u>May I present to you... *drum roll*... My Jesse!</u>
  </pre>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397504i/767078._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Holy sh!t to the crazy man - Jesse. And Ava sweetie...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380374435ra/728461.gif" width="300" height="169" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b> Before I start can I have a moment please?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397504ra/767079.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Theeeeeeere much better... now on to the review </b><br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~<br><br><br>Let's start off with presenting the Manor of Jesse... simply beautiful and well I dare you to take an ungaurded peak into one of the rooms (whoops... I did not say that)<br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397504i/767081._SX540_.jpg" width="440" height="277" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The beautiful, young and talented interior decorator Ava O'Shea heads out to Manor only for a consult but gets so much more. From the moment their eyes meet there is crazy chemistry (and I mean crazy!). Chemistry you feel thick in the air and as Ava's friend, Kate, said chemistry that gets YOU horny if you are in proximity.<br><br>A much older, successful *cough* hotel owner &amp; manager, Jesse, wants her and pulls out all the stops... and I mean it! the man goes over the top crazy to get Jesse. In a real world I would have been withdrawing my accounts and visiting some shady businesses to get a new identity. Then getting off the grid far away as possible from this man. But thank god this man is a figment imagination of this brilliant writer. <b>Seriously,</b> I hope this wasn't modeled after someone.<br><br>Gotta say there is not much happening for most of the book... mostly it's just *SEMI-SPOILER ALERT* hot sex, short dresses, drunken escapades, non-stop ringing phones, cussing, temper tantrums and JEEZ THE NON-STOP CAT AND MOUSE CHASE GAMES.<br><br>There is quiet a lot not being said... like Jesse's age... seriously with all this mystery he better be a well preserved man in his 60's lol.<br>I really wish we had more on his past, too. I think at 70% I was getting exasperated that we weren't getting shit. Hopefully book 2?<br><br>Perhaps we can get bit of a backbone for Ava, while we at it. Seriously girl, he is going all loco on you and you are scared to ask him the hard questions. Jeez half of the time you are doubting yourself and grow cold on him when he says a wrong word that does not belong in your perfect HEA world. Grow up! Can't you tell he is a fucked up millionaire with some messed up past hmm?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397504ra/767082.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>Btw, who want to kills this Sarah bitch with me? Who is she???<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397504ra/767083.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>Now the ending...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397504ra/767084.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>hopefully that is all in that and I can't wait to get to book 2. Hopefully Ava learned some things and found her voice.<br><br>Those two are explosive but they belong together no doubt.<br><blockquote>
  <i> 'He brings out the worst in me too. He hates me swearing, so I do it more. he has issues with exposing my flesh to anyone other than him, so I wear shorter dresses. he tells me not to get drunk, so I do...'</i>
</blockquote><br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Lady, you're mine forever"</i>
</blockquote><br><br><div>

  <u> Random Ramblings:</u>
</b><br> - The man sure loves his toppings and condiments... Whip Cream, PB, Chocolate, Ava lol<br> - So many different type of sex: catching-up sex, reminder fuck, sense fuck, retribution fuck, sleepy sex, apology fuck, hangover sex... hm... am I missing anything more from this book?<br><br><b> Favorite quote </b><br><blockquote>
  <i>The modern man needs to catch on to the fact that women want to be treated as equals, but only when it suits us. the modern woman's fierce need for independence doesn't mean we want to pay for our half of a meal, or that we don't want a man to hold a door open for us. We still want to be looked after, but on our terms.</i>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer462556642" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11456656808776406225">REREAD on March 17-19,2018;<br/>I decided to give this series a re-read considering book #4 is coming out soon! My memory isn't what it used to be, so I want to make sure I have all the details freshly in my mind! It is also kind of neat to see how my tastes and opinions have changed over the years! In the case of Jesse Ward and Ava, I will say that my opinions do still stand; although I have way more tolerance for Jesse's stalkerish tendencies and his possessiveness. A part of the reason for that is</span>
  <span id="freeText11456656808776406225" style="display:none">REREAD on March 17-19,2018;<br />I decided to give this series a re-read considering book #4 is coming out soon! My memory isn't what it used to be, so I want to make sure I have all the details freshly in my mind! It is also kind of neat to see how my tastes and opinions have changed over the years! In the case of Jesse Ward and Ava, I will say that my opinions do still stand; although I have way more tolerance for Jesse's stalkerish tendencies and his possessiveness. A part of the reason for that is I have read some very dark reads since I have read this series....and Jesse doesn't seem near as bad as some of the anti-heroes I have recently read about! LOL I will say that Ava ticked me off more this time around. With her hot and cold attitude, and always leaving him...I would have kicked her to the curb...Just saying. She must be really hot in bed for him to put up with her...LOL <br /><br />What I noticed this time around as well is that a lot of the recent books don't even compare to the intensity of Jesse and Ava's relationship. Their passion as well, is so hard to beat. They just don't make books like they used to!!! I think it is time for me to revisit some of my other faves over time, because truly it is rare for me to be hooked on stories now like I was back then! Moving on to book #2!! Ava had better be nicer to Jesse, or I am going to start not liking her! LOL<br /><br /><br /><br />Original Review from 2013:<br /><br /><br />I have some very mixed feelings when it comes to this book. I have to say that a big part of the book made me feel uncomfortable with the way Jesse treated Ava. I normally LOVE alpha males and even enjoy them controlling their woman! Jesse took control to a new level that, in my opinion; was extremely abusive. Ava was not happy with him "bossing" her around, but usually she would just let him have his own way, which again rubbed me the wrong way. At one point, he punches a hole in Ava's roomates door, and when the roomate comes back and sees it, Jesse throws her a bunch of money to fix it and then everything is ok...UH HELLO???? What am I missing here??? Where on earth is this type of behaviour acceptable, and further more how is that romantic?? Jesse had also MAJOR stalking tendencies, and a huge issue with Ava wearing revealing clothes. He also holds a lot of information about himself inside and doesnt' share with Ava, so she never really gets to know him and his personal life. She doesn't even know how old he is!<br />Now, in saying all of this, I still gave this book a four star rating and this is why I felt it deserved it! The sex in this book is beyond HOT! It is so intense and holy smoly!!!! I had to fan myself on several occasions! The author knows how to write a sex scene like nobody's business!!! Whether we were treated to "Sleepy Sex", "Possessive Sex" or even his famous "Sense Sex", there was no shortage of steamy scenes in this story! This is one of the hottest books I have read in a long time! So for all of my complaints, I still was hooked onto the pages and the explosive ending had me extremely glad that I had waited to read this story until the second book was available! Believe me, as soon as I finished this one, I immediately began the next installment!! I am strongly hoping that the next book will reveal more of why Jesse is the way he is, and of course I am expecting that we will be highly entertained with intense rip roaring hot sex!!!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16893225812216756253"><b>4-ish CRAZY-ass Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397477ra/767006.gif' width='480' height='360' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"I’m keeping you forever."</i>
</b><br/><br/>Really,really glad I read this story!! I understand now the controversial reviews and why few DNF, but I kinda loved it. It's nothing unique really. But it's funny, it's bat-shit crazy, it's enjoying. My kinda of sexy read! <br/><br/>And all of you sexy billionaires, you think you are insane? Possesive? Ha, ha, ha..<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397477ra/767007.gif' width='500' height='281' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>There is a a new psychotic man in town. And he deserves to be hospitalized!!!!!!!!!! THIS MAN!<br/><br/>So, WELCOME TO <b>THE MANOR</b><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Seriously</span></span>
  <span id="freeText16893225812216756253" style="display:none"><b>4-ish CRAZY-ass Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397477ra/767006.gif" width="480" height="360" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"I’m keeping you forever."</i>
</b><br><br>Really,really glad I read this story!! I understand now the controversial reviews and why few DNF, but I kinda loved it. It's nothing unique really. But it's funny, it's bat-shit crazy, it's enjoying. My kinda of sexy read! <br><br>And all of you sexy billionaires, you think you are insane? Possesive? Ha, ha, ha..<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397477ra/767007.gif" width="500" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There is a a new psychotic man in town. And he deserves to be hospitalized!!!!!!!!!! THIS MAN!<br><br>So, WELCOME TO <b>THE MANOR</b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Seriously, who didn't immediately thought that this was a sex club.... <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381660096i/5154845.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Every manor has a Lord and Master and ours is the one and only:<br><blockquote>
  <b>Jesse Ward</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Jesse is insane. Don't get me wrong... I love him completely but he is arrogant, jealous, possessive, flawed, liar, filthy rich, adrenaline junkie. Cavemann Style!!!!!!!!! He is interesting to read, keeps you on your toes, AMAZING! I don't suggest marrying him, but admiring from a safe distance? DEFINITELY!<br><br><b>
  <i>"I’m going to possess every.single.part.of.you. He punctuates each word clearly and sharply. There will be nowhere on this beautiful body that won’t have had me in it, on it or over it."</i>
</b><br><br>Our unsuspecting heroine is Ava O'Shea. <br><br><b>
  <i>"I’m not getting caught up with a handsome stranger, no matter how handsome he is. And oh, is he mind meltingly delicious. Anyway, he’s way too old for me. And more importantly, he’s obviously taken. And that only reinforces the fact that he’s an ultimate player. This is not the sort of man I need to be attracted to, damn me, especially after Matt and his infidelities. I need a man, eventually, who’ll be faithful, protective and look after me – preferably a bit nearer my age too."</i>
</b><br><br>No awkward bone in her body... A young accomplished designer, opinionated, some issues with an ex, but a real coward. The only thing it kinda went old with this story is the summary of Jesse and Ava's relationship...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397477i/767009.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I swear, every 20 damn pages, she was running away! Constantly! I wanted to tie her up and spank her!!!!!!!!!! I was FED UP!<br>Yeap girl, Jesse has some serious issues but you can't hide your head in the sand, you are amazing together!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397477ra/767010.gif" width="400" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And by the end, she drove him over the edge (not that he wasn't close..) and everything crashed and burned and we left them in ruins... <br>WHAT THE HELL?!?!?!?!?! One of the worst cliffhangers endings I have ever read!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397477ra/767011.gif" width="500" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Thank God I waited until now to read it. The next is to be released next week, so I can handle it!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/648948.gif" width="500" height="276" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Also what I really liked in this book, was the glimpse into the modern womanhood and how that clashes with our basic female instincts. It is something that me (and probably enough of you) struggles with every day. Our hard-won independence or the alpha male. The answer is as always somewhere in-between...<br><br><b>
  <i>"The modern man needs to catch on to the fact that women want to be treated as equals, but only when it suits us. The modern woman’s fierce need for independence doesn’t mean we want to pay for our half of a meal, or that we don’t want a man to hold a door open for us. We still want to be looked after, but on our terms."</i>
</b><br><br><i>Painful admittion: I was on date and the clown I was with, broke out the calculator and told me that my half of the meal was 12,23 EUROS... True and painful story!! I, of course gave him 25 EUROS, stormed off and bribed my brother to make him a call...LOL! Great times!</i> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397477ra/767012.gif" width="500" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>If you are looking for the ultimate male, look no further... An intense read I really enjoyed! I have already started the countdown for the next!<b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/417407.gif" width="499" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></b></b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_458015654" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/458015654" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/458015654?book_show_action=true">Nov 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer458015654" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11571359344418741565"><br/><b>3.5 CRAZY, POSSESSIVE, <i>"WATCH YOUR MOUTH"</i> STARS.</b><br/><br/><br/><b>Who <i>is</i> This Man??</b><br/><br/>Let me provide you with a mental image first...<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397958i/768538._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>We know his name is <b>Jesse Ward</b>.<br/><br/>We know that YES, Jesse is pretty much perfect on the outside... He's dangerously handsome, filthy rich and he's also the Lord of the Manor; a blooming, successful "hotel" for which Jesse has hired the 26 year old ambitious interior designer <b>Ava O'Shea</b> to redesign some of the rooms.<br/><br/>From the moment Ava and Jesse meet, there's an instant powerful connection</span>
  <span id="freeText11571359344418741565" style="display:none"><br><b>3.5 CRAZY, POSSESSIVE, <i>"WATCH YOUR MOUTH"</i> STARS.</b><br><br><br><b>Who <i>is</i> This Man??</b><br><br>Let me provide you with a mental image first...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397958i/768538._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We know his name is <b>Jesse Ward</b>.<br><br>We know that YES, Jesse is pretty much perfect on the outside... He's dangerously handsome, filthy rich and he's also the Lord of the Manor; a blooming, successful "hotel" for which Jesse has hired the 26 year old ambitious interior designer <b>Ava O'Shea</b> to redesign some of the rooms.<br><br>From the moment Ava and Jesse meet, there's an instant powerful connection between and they're immediately attracted to each other. Or, as Ava's friend Kate said it: <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Ava, the sexual tension batting between you and that man was so fucking super charged, even I was horny!"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Ava tries to stay away from the mysterious businessman because she KNOWS he has "heartbreak" written all over him but there's no escaping a guy like Jesse... He's the kind of guy who ALWAYS gets what he wants.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Just tell me one thing before you leave, Ava." His voice prickles at my senses, and I find my eyes travelling up the leanness of his body until our stares meet. His face is serious, but still stunning. "How loud do you think you'll scream when I fuck you?"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>First off, what I would like to say to Jesse: <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397958i/768539.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>I mean, the guy has some serious control issues, he pretty much takes being a control freak to the extreme... And most of the things he does would practically drive any sane woman INSANE. And if he doesn't get what he wants, he uses all kinds of methods, most of them including sex, to get his way.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You'll always need me, Ava. I'm going to make sure of it. Now, let's see if we can fuck some sense into you."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Then there's the infamous phrase he likes to use so much: <i>"Watch your fucking mouth"</i>. He uses it ALL the time whenever Ava accidently uses a cuss word, he uses it while they're arguing, while they're having sex, while they're jogging in the park... Seriously, by 50 % into the story I was starting to get extremely exasperated with hearing him say that...<p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397958ra/768540.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p> Especially, since he had NO PROBLEM at all when <i>he</i> was the one swearing (which he did a lot of times for that matter).<br><br><br><b>The story</b> of Ava and Jesse basically consists of them getting together, then they have some huge argument (mostly whenever Ava didn't want to do things exactly the way Jesse wanted her to), she tries to run away from him, he chases after her (resulting in a lot of banging on doors and an endless amount of phone calls), they get back together. And the cycle repeats itself...<br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397958ra/768541.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br>I know, it all seems a little shallow and predictable and admittedly, at times I thought it was just that BUT the last 30 % of the story changed my opinion about that. Things started to get much more interesting and there were some surprising revelations that make me anxious to find out how the story will continue...<br><br>So, despite all of Jesse's craziness, will I still continue reading the rest of the series??<br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/583939.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p> Granted, Jesse was HOT and he could also be really sweet sometimes...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Is that all you rang for?" "No, I wanted to hear your voice." he says softly. "I'm having Ava withdrawal."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Also, there are just so many unanswered questions about Jesse's past that I can't wait to find out and then there's the <u>main unsolved mystery</u>: <i>"Exactly how old is he????"</i><br><br>If you're going to read this book, prepare yourself for some very frustrating confrontations and for the intensity that is Jesse Ward... Overall, I ended up really enjoying <i>This Man</i> and because of the (not so pleasant) cliffhanger, I'll definitely start the second part of this series <i>Beneath This Man</i> soon.<br><br><br><br>****<br><br><br><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="11571359344418741565" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_457284338" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/457284338" />
    <a title="Holly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2127955-holly"><img alt="Holly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1520179670p2/2127955.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/457284338?book_show_action=true">Nov 16, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Holly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Holly" href="/user/show/2127955-holly">Holly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2127955-holly?shelf=hot-mess">hot-mess</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2127955-holly?shelf=books-that-make-you-go-wtf">books-that-make-you-go-wtf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2127955-holly?shelf=e-book">e-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2127955-holly?shelf=2012">2012</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer457284338" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11082529131472481658">Attempting to write a review for this book without allowing myself to go off on a rant about everything that bothered me about the story would be next to impossible. So, consider yourself warned.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397848ra/768093.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>I am a fan of the Alpha Male character in books. Hell, gimme an Uber-Alpha Male and I'm an even happier girl. But...there is a difference between being an Alpha Male and being an obnoxious bully. Sometimes the lines blur, but in the case of this book...there is no question that the character of Jesse War</span>
  <span id="freeText11082529131472481658" style="display:none">Attempting to write a review for this book without allowing myself to go off on a rant about everything that bothered me about the story would be next to impossible. So, consider yourself warned.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397848ra/768093.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I am a fan of the Alpha Male character in books. Hell, gimme an Uber-Alpha Male and I'm an even happier girl. But...there is a difference between being an Alpha Male and being an obnoxious bully. Sometimes the lines blur, but in the case of this book...there is no question that the character of Jesse Ward is a first class asshat.<br><br>Let me make this clear: There is nothing sexy about Jesse's behavior in this book. Nothing. He becomes obsessed with and begins systematically stalking Ava after their first encounter. Calling her phone dozens of times and when she refuses to answer he goes out and gets a new cell phone so he can trick her by calling her from another phone number. Showing up at her house in the middle of the night, banging on her door and screaming like a madman until she lets him in. Calling and blowing up at her for not calling him as soon as she got home after spending the night with him (oh, and did I mention the fact that she wanted to return home the night before but he physically restrained her from leaving?). I'm sorry, but if someone acted like that in real life, his ass would get arrested pretty damn quick.<br><br>As far as the sex scenes go...I am far from a prude. In fact a large portion of the books I have read in 2012 have been erotica &amp; BDSM related. Having said that, in my opinion there is nothing sexy about basically forcing a particular sex act on someone regardless of the fact that the woman 'ended up liking it'. After that scene it became increasingly difficult for me to continue on to the end of this book.<br><br>Oh, and did i mention how Malpas described Jesse as being twitchy, having clammy hands and having a habit of heavy breathing on Ava?!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397848ra/768094.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As others have mentioned, this book is by an independent British author who continually uses many British terms that are unfamiliar. I can pretty much ignore that most of the time and something like that very rarely makes me enjoy a good book less. However, here I found myself downright confused at times. Ava <b>repeatedly</b> describes Jesse's eyes as being "sludgy". Now, I am assuming that the author meant this in a positive way (considering she uses the term when Ava is waxing poetic about how impossibly perfect Jesse is), but it just didn't compute with me. Maybe's it's some obscure British-ism, but it was especially distracting given how many times the author used the term. <br><br>Speaking of which...and I feel like I'm having a <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10818853.Fifty_Shades_of_Grey__Fifty_Shades___1_" title="Fifty Shades of Grey (Fifty Shades, #1) by E.L. James" rel="nofollow noopener">Fifty Shades of Grey</a> flashback here, but this author was extremely repetitive. Jesse was continually yelling at Ava about cursing ("Watch your mouth, lady!") even while cursing himself. And dear Lord in heaven I think I speak for everyone who read this book when I ask the following question:<br><br><b>
  <i>HOW OLD IS JESSE WARD???!!!???</i>
</b><br><br>I really wish the author had cleared that up because I was so damn sick of Ava pontificating about it throughout the book. In the beginning, Ava comments that Jesse looks to be in his early 30's, but at other times she acts like he is a dirty old man and must be in his 40's or 50's because she constantly comments about how much older he is than her (even though she is in her mid 20's). That was just one more aspect of the story line that I found maddening.<br><br>Despite what it might sound like given the tone of this review, I did go into this book with an open mind, wanting to like it. Unfortunately it was 100% not for me.<br><br>Read more reviews at my blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://ravingbookaddict.blogspot.com/">http://ravingbookaddict.blogspot.com/</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="11082529131472481658" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_454107108" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/454107108" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/454107108?book_show_action=true">Nov 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=smuttastic">smuttastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=shower-smexin">shower-smexin</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=super-rich-hero">super-rich-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=scarred-heroes">scarred-heroes</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer454107108" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13936830075853506923">It was with no small amount of trepidation that I embarked upon this novel. After reading hugely differing opinions on the hero and the writing in general in reviews, I was concerned that this story was going to wave all sorts of personal red flags for me, rake up painful memories and generally traumatise me. Thankfully, this caution was most definitely misplaced as I very much enjoyed this book – in fact, I loved every second.<br/><br/>It’s the story of interior designer Ava, a girl about town, in London</span>
  <span id="freeText13936830075853506923" style="display:none">It was with no small amount of trepidation that I embarked upon this novel. After reading hugely differing opinions on the hero and the writing in general in reviews, I was concerned that this story was going to wave all sorts of personal red flags for me, rake up painful memories and generally traumatise me. Thankfully, this caution was most definitely misplaced as I very much enjoyed this book – in fact, I loved every second.<br><br>It’s the story of interior designer Ava, a girl about town, in London. She is asked to go to The Manor, a ‘hotel’ in the Surrey foothills to quote on a redesign for some of their rooms. The minute she meets the owner, Jesse Ward, there is an instant, physical attraction sparking between them. Ava can hardly function, she’s so flustered by the impossibly handsome Mr Ward and he feels the same way about her but manages to remain far calmer. He pursues her and they embark upon an emotionally exhausting relationship. All the time that I was reading this, I was waiting for the ‘big bad’ that would make me hate Jesse but it never came. He is kind of outrageous but I found a lot to love.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>‘Just tell me one thing before you leave, Ava.’ His voice prickles at my senses, and I find my eyes travelling up the leanness of his body until our stares meet. His face is serious, but still stunning. ‘How loud do you think you’ll scream when I fuck you?’</blockquote>
</b><br><br>So, Jesse Ward. Mr Ward is quite the enigma.<br><br><a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397366i/766670._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Jesse is devastatingly handsome, he towers over her, kisses her on the cheek and generally puts her under his spell right from the very first second she claps eyes on him. Despite her initial reluctance as she thinks he already has a girlfriend, Jesse aggressively pursues Ava, almost forcing her into a relationship. He reduced her to a quivering mass of lust and sexual awareness, using her desire to coerce her into his arms. He’s aggressive, unreasonable, challenging, protective, possessive, moody, temperamental and an absolute control freak. There’s almost a desperation to him as he endeavours to keep Ava within arm’s reach at all times, to keep her from her normal routine and friends, to completely take over her life. He appears mortally afraid that he will lose her but yet he just demands these things of her, attempts to control her but will never open up and tell her why.<br><br>He’s keeping so many secrets – he won’t tell her his real age, he has a prominent jagged scar across his abdomen that he won’t explain and he certainly won’t tell her what is really going on at The Manor. He’s so possessive – he tells her relentlessly that she’s his but he never confesses his true feelings. One second, he talks about them being together forever and the next he tells her that they’re just fucking. With such uncertainty, Ava decides not to confess to Jesse that she is in love with him.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>I drop my head. I can’t look at him. What can I tell him? That I’ve fallen in love with him? Perhaps I should – he might freak out and leave me alone. I shrug instead.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Ava is a great heroine – I really enjoyed reading her story. It’s so nice to have a British author set the story firmly in London – everything is authentic and Ava’s lifestyle is spot on the way a 20something single girl is, working the 9-5 in London, getting drunk on the weekend with her friends and work colleagues, going to pubs and clubs, shopping in Camden. This is just exactly how it is and it lends an air of reality to the whole story.<br><br>I think I’d have to put this one in the erotic romance category because there is a whole lotta lovin going on. Jesse and Ava share an exquisitely intense physical connection as they steam up the pages of the story with their sex scenes – there’s sense fucks, reminder fucks, rebound fucks, hangover sex, sleepy sex – all with perfectly synchronised orgasms. Perfect 10’s every single time. OK, so that is all highly unrealistic but it sure makes for pleasurable reading!!<br><br>So, I think I understand why so many reviewers had problems with the hero – he is most definitely a bit of a jerk but the story’s so compelling to me and that’s what I’m judging this book on. Jesse may be a bit of an idiot but it sure makes for a captivating and engrossing story and you know I’ll be waiting with bated breath for the upcoming sequel on January 18th as there is still a long way to go yet.<br><br>So, if you like an uber-alpha, dominant, controlling, obnoxious yet very handsome hero who is shit hot in bed and a taut, emotionally exhausting, intense romance, I think you might well enjoy this book. Give it a go and come back and tell me what you thought.<br><br>4.5 stars batshit crazy romance<br><br><i>For more reviews, please visit <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="13936830075853506923" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer9696751913492116777"><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"Met the Lord, have we?"</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br/>Another reread for one of my favourite series, and surprisingly and shyly I have to confess that I still have not overcome my crush on Jesse Ward.<br/><br/><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"Oh good God. My heart crashes against my breast bone and my nervous breathing rockets to damn right dangerous levels. I suddenly feel light headed, and my mouth is ignoring my brains instructions to at least say <u>something</u>. I just stand there staring at this man, while he stares back at me. His husky voice ha</blockquote></b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText9696751913492116777" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"Met the Lord, have we?"</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br />Another reread for one of my favourite series, and surprisingly and shyly I have to confess that I still have not overcome my crush on Jesse Ward.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"Oh good God. My heart crashes against my breast bone and my nervous breathing rockets to damn right dangerous levels. I suddenly feel light headed, and my mouth is ignoring my brains instructions to at least say <u>something</u>. I just stand there staring at this man, while he stares back at me. His husky voice halted me in my tracks, but the sight of him... well, that's just turned me into a non-responsive quivering wreck."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br />What a story! This book was brilliant. I loved it and I got hooked from the first until the last page. <br /><br />This is a book full of passion and extreme emotions. Two people will fall in love and during this process there is a lot of chasing and a lot of yelling. <br />And this is the oldest game in flirting/mating in the history of human kind. The woman runs away and the man runs after her. Sometimes they shout and fight with each other, but in the end they have make up sex and all is good. This is completely natural and funny. It is just a game of two people who are crazy for each other from the first moment their eyes meet.<br /><br />The book is full of twists and secrets which come out at some point. The only sure fact is that Jesse is ALMOST NEVER honest with Ava. <br />Another fact is that he wants her like crazy and he will do anything, I repeat HE WILL DO ANYTHING to have her and to keep her.<br /><br />Ava behaves like a reluctant virgin towards Jesse and this is something he will make her stop it during the first 10 minutes they spend in the bathroom of his new flat and the first half an hour they spend in the kitchen of his old flat.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>Ava, you should know that once I've had you, you're mine.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br />And the big questions are three:<br />1. What is happening with Ava's pills? Why they keep disappearing?<br />2. How old is Jesse? Seriously only 19?<br />3. Why the mansion/hotel does not have a front desk and sightseeing brochures?<br /><br />I am sure all the people who are reading the book will suspect the answers to these questions before the book finishes. Only Ava does not seem to realise what is going on around her since she is lost somewhere inside Central Jesse's Cloud 9.</span>

</b> This book DID have a solid plot..it's just that I found the book a tad bit predictable for my taste.Found the chracters either a bit to whiney or too aggressive with each other.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428168267ra/14380440.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>Would I recommend this book ? </b>
</i><br>Not really.No<br><br><i>
  <b>Will I be reading the sequal ? </b>
